  <div class=\"bg-white padd-all-10\">\n                            <div class=\"row text-left\">\n                              <div class=\"col-md-12\">\n                                <p>\n                                  </p><h4>Travel Agency Incentives Program</h4>\n                                <p></p>\n                                <p>\n                                                         Interjet is pleased to introduce its Travel Agency Incentives Program.  Under this program, registered travel agencies will be eligible to receive incentive credits, which may be used towards the purchase of air transportation.  Incentive tickets may be purchased on any of interjet´s domestic or international routes, without blackout dates or seat inventory restrictions.  \n                                                    </p>\n                                <p>\n                                  </p><h4>Terms and Conditions:</h4>\n                                <p></p>\n                                <p>\n                                  </p><ul>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    Travel agencies and their authorized travel agents wishing to participate in this program must register online through Interjet´s Agency Jet module. Only ticket issued through a registered Agency Jet account will be eligible for incentives.  \n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    Travel Agency may register Travel Agent accounts under its main organization ID. Accumulated monthly sales from all accounts will be assigned to the Agency´s main account. \n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    Monthly sales cut-off date will be the 1st day of the following month. \n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li> \n                                                                    Incentives are calculated over the base fare; taxes and fees excluded.  \n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    Interjet will deposit accrued monthly incentive credits into a separate Agency E-Wallet account on the 15th of the following month.  The accrued balance can be viewed, and incentive credits redeemed through the Agency Incentive account. \n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    The monthly incentives will be valid for 90 days from the date of deposit into the Agency´s E-Wallet account.  In the event that the incentives are not used by the corresponding validity date; the credit will be canceled and removed from the account.   \n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    Incentive credits may not be redeemed for cash or any other form of financial means. Credits may be applied towards the purchase of airline tickets´ fare base only.  Taxes and fees must be paid with a credit card as form of payment. \n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    Tickets purchased with incentive credits are not eligible for new incentives accrual.\n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    Interjet reserves the right to modify or cancel its Agency Jet Incentive Program, in which instance it will notify 24 hours in advance through the Agency Jet module.\n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    Intertours and Ground Transportation Services (Interjet by Ground) are not eligible for accrual of incentives under this program.\n                                                               </li>\n                                    <li>\n                                                                    The incentives will be calculated in accordance to the dollar amount of tickets purchased on a monthly basis.  For more details, consult with your local Sales Representative.\n                                                               </li>\n                                  </ul>\n
